name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Executive Studio Apartment
info:Stayed in April 2023
info:Family
info:13 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted May 2, 2023
msg:This hotel is in a great location, and breakfast is pretty nice. The staff were friendly and helpful. The room had a well-equipped small kitchen area. Highline restaurant is really nice.

A few downsides:
1. We stayed here in the spring (May), when the weather was pretty warm, and they were turning their air conditioning off in the rooms every day from 8pm to 10am. This means we were a bit hot at night. They provided a fan, but it was still warm. This is clearly just a cost-cutting measure but they should adjust when the weather gets warm. And many guests may like to sleep in cooler temperatures even when the weather is not that warm outside.
2. Their hotel was pretty full for the holiday, so they ran out of extra blankets. We had our kids with us and paid for an extra bed, so we were expecting to be able to get blankets from the hotel but couldn't do so (since the room was so warm, though, we just got an extra sheet and did okay with that.
3. The description of the executive studio room says it has a sofa. We thought one of our kids could sleep on it. But it is not a sofa, it is just an armchair, so no one can sleep on it.
4. The first night we stayed there, I think there was a party going on in Highline restaurant in the hotel and the music was very loud. We were 14 floors above the restaurant but could still hear the bass coming through, which was annoying and made it difficult to go to sleep.
----------------------------------------
